The outcome of Martyrs on Wednesday was 68 martyrs, most of them in Aleppo, were 15 martyrs killed in Jarablos and 8 martyrs in Ritan during clashes with "Dae'sh" in Aleppo as elevated martyrs in Yarmouk refugee camp, as a result of food shortages and Two martyrs in Hamouriah as a result of bombing in Damascus . Between martyrs 4 women , 4 children and 5 martyrs under torture
Aleppo : 34, including 3 children and a woman * Damascus and its countryside : 14, including a woman and a child, 3 martyrs under torture * Idlib : 6, including a martyr under torture * Daraa : 5 * Homs : 4, including Two women
Hama : 4, including a martyr under torture
